467|e12632|        /// PERFORMANCE: Visible-range-only highlighting for very large files
468|5ae4eb|        /// Only highlights the text that's currently visible on screen, dramatically reducing lag
469|1745ca|        func applyVisibleRangeHighlighting(to textView: UITextView) {
470|8ebaf1|            guard !isApplyingHighlighting else { return }
471|cfeb02|            isApplyingHighlighting = true
472|3070d1|            
473|b3d375|            let text = textView.text ?? ""
474|4664a0|            let filename = parent.filename
475|6035ba|            let theme = ThemeManager.shared.currentTheme
476|810685|            let fontSize = parent.editorCore.editorFontSize
477|e844dd|            let selectedRange = textView.selectedRange
478|3070d1|            
479|f6efe3|            // Calculate visible range with buffer
480|6229cc|            let visibleRect = textView.bounds
481|349839|            let textContainer = textView.textContainer
482|d8c2f5|            let layoutManager = textView.layoutManager
483|3070d1|            
484|0c5215|            // Get the glyph range for the visible rect
485|ae7522|            var visibleGlyphRange = NSRange()
486|d7414d|            layoutManager.enumerateLineFragments(forGlyphRange: NSRange(location: 0, length: layoutManager.numberOfGlyphs)) { (rect, usedRect, container, glyphRange, stop) in
487|f88a67|                if rect.intersects(visibleRect) {
488|1abb87|                    if visibleGlyphRange.length == 0 {
489|050ceb|                        visibleGlyphRange = glyphRange
490|540066|                    } else {
491|cd3ba9|                        visibleGlyphRange.length = glyphRange.location + glyphRange.length - visibleGlyphRange.location
492|c9717a|                    }
493|5c545a|                } else if visibleGlyphRange.length > 0 && rect.minY > visibleRect.maxY {
494|bee479|                    stop.pointee = true
495|4e2d32|                }
496|a7dc16|            }
497|3070d1|            
498|41d44a|            // Convert glyph range to character range
499|16db73|            var visibleCharRange = layoutManager.characterRange(forGlyphRange: visibleGlyphRange, actualGlyphRange: nil)
500|3070d1|            
501|5fccb8|            // Add buffer of ~50 lines before and after for smooth scrolling
502|5b9a15|            let bufferChars = 5000
503|951c81|            let rangeStart = max(0, visibleCharRange.location - bufferChars)
504|e91e65|            let rangeEnd = min(text.utf16.count, visibleCharRange.location + visibleCharRange.length + bufferChars)
505|0a73c6|            visibleCharRange = NSRange(location: rangeStart, length: rangeEnd - rangeStart)
506|3070d1|            
507|403160|            // Process highlighting on background thread
508|f7a14b|            DispatchQueue.global(qos: .userInitiated).async { [weak self] in
509|ca0cbb|                // Extract the visible portion of text
510|c31673|                let nsText = text as NSString
511|90d016|                let safeRange = NSRange(
512|d26358|                    location: visibleCharRange.location,
513|b8f958|                    length: min(visibleCharRange.length, nsText.length - visibleCharRange.location)
514|6f642e|                )
515|bcd97e|                guard safeRange.length > 0 else {
516|586632|                    DispatchQueue.main.async {
517|16bdbd|                        self?.isApplyingHighlighting = false
518|c9717a|                    }
519|d253ab|                    return
520|4e2d32|                }
521|216278|                
522|3969c2|                let visibleText = nsText.substring(with: safeRange)
523|216278|                
524|58d54c|                // Highlight only the visible portion
525|fe758b|                let highlighter = VSCodeSyntaxHighlighter(theme: theme, fontSize: fontSize)
526|2de969|                let highlightedVisible = highlighter.highlight(visibleText, filename: filename)
527|216278|                
528|351cca|                // Apply on main thread
529|f143b8|                DispatchQueue.main.async {
530|9e6003|                    guard let self = self else { return }
531|b4f836|                    self.isApplyingHighlighting = false
532|dd2193|                    
533|a5d572|                    // Only apply if text hasn't changed while we were processing
534|1eb7d3|                    guard textView.text == text else { return }
535|dd2193|                    
536|f3a98b|                    // Create full attributed string with base styling
537|a42544|                    let fullAttributed = NSMutableAttributedString(string: text)
538|87360e|                    let baseFont = UIFont.monospacedSystemFont(ofSize: fontSize, weight: .regular)
539|268dc5|                    let baseColor = UIColor(theme.editorForeground)
540|a055f2|                    let fullRange = NSRange(location: 0, length: text.utf16.count)
541|321bcf|                    fullAttributed.addAttribute(.font, value: baseFont, range: fullRange)
542|06d443|                    fullAttributed.addAttribute(.foregroundColor, value: baseColor, range: fullRange)
543|dd2193|                    
544|523d33|                    // Apply highlighted attributes only to visible range
545|08c21f|                    highlightedVisible.enumerateAttributes(in: NSRange(location: 0, length: highlightedVisible.length), options: []) { attrs, range, _ in
546|70612a|                        let targetRange = NSRange(location: safeRange.location + range.location, length: range.length)
547|a7f982|                        if targetRange.location + targetRange.length <= fullAttributed.length {
548|0cc493|                            for (key, value) in attrs {
549|430195|                                fullAttributed.addAttribute(key, value: value, range: targetRange)
550|89d40a|                            }
551|392b35|                        }
552|c9717a|                    }
553|dd2193|                    
554|3140c3|                    textView.attributedText = fullAttributed
555|0602f2|                    textView.selectedRange = selectedRange
556|dd2193|                    
557|5446e6|                    textView.typingAttributes = [
558|e5800b|                        .font: baseFont,
559|beaa64|                        .foregroundColor: baseColor
560|3b8c65|                    ]
561|dd2193|                    
562|3f20cb|                    self.lastThemeId = theme.id
563|4e2d32|                }
564|a7dc16|            }
565|5f3077|        }

52|0a2291|        blinkTimer?.invalidate()
53|27e597|    }
54|adc83b|
55|aff961|    private func setupCursorBlinking() {
56|2c9899|        blinkTimer = Timer.scheduledTimer(withTimeInterval: 0.5, repeats: true) { [weak self] _ in
57|7b2278|            self?.cursorVisible.toggle()
58|bfc77d|            self?.updateCursorVisibility()
59|5f3077|        }
60|27e597|    }
61|adc83b|
62|0cd67c|    private func updateCursorVisibility() {
63|51f629|        let alpha: Float = cursorVisible ? 1.0 : 0.0
64|b8b14f|        cursorLayers.forEach { $0.opacity = alpha }
65|27e597|    }
66|adc83b|
67|0532f5|    /// Updates the display of all cursors and selections
68|5f61b8|    func updateCursorDisplay() {
69|1b261a|        // Remove existing cursor and selection layers
70|36b44e|        cursorLayers.forEach { $0.removeFromSuperlayer() }
71|bb580b|        cursorLayers.removeAll()
72|a50cf9|        selectionLayers.forEach { $0.removeFromSuperlayer() }
73|582ae4|        selectionLayers.removeAll()
74|adc83b|
75|2ffb0a|        guard let editorCore = editorCore else { return }
76|15f135|        let cursors = editorCore.multiCursorState.cursors
77|adc83b|
78|a202cd|        // Only show additional cursors if we have multiple
79|71f1cc|        guard cursors.count > 1 else { return }
80|adc83b|
81|72ad69|        // Draw each cursor (skip the primary one as UITextView handles it)
82|16631c|        for (index, cursor) in cursors.enumerated() {
83|933ac1|            // Draw selection if present
84|94aef6|            if let selectionRange = cursor.selectionRange {
85|1d74b0|                drawSelection(for: selectionRange, isPrimary: cursor.isPrimary, index: index)
86|a7dc16|            }
87|adc83b|
88|c6cef0|            // Draw cursor line (skip primary cursor as system handles it)
89|bb0725|            if !cursor.isPrimary {
90|a10f1a|                drawCursor(at: cursor.position, isPrimary: false, index: index)
91|a7dc16|            }
92|5f3077|        }
93|27e597|    }
94|adc83b|
95|eb46c0|    private func drawCursor(at position: Int, isPrimary: Bool, index: Int) {
96|11ce2b|        guard let textPosition = self.position(from: beginningOfDocument, offset: position) else { return }
97|adc83b|
98|b34ecc|        let caretRect = self.caretRect(for: textPosition)
99|adc83b|
100|037254|        let cursorLayer = CALayer()
101|dc404a|        cursorLayer.backgroundColor = (isPrimary ? cursorColor : secondaryCursorColor).cgColor
102|66be0e|        cursorLayer.frame = CGRect(
103|0270b6|            x: caretRect.origin.x,
104|b56626|            y: caretRect.origin.y,
105|122136|            width: cursorWidth,
106|2f842a|            height: caretRect.height
107|3143a4|        )
108|8e5363|        cursorLayer.cornerRadius = 1
109|adc83b|
110|06cd55|        layer.addSublayer(cursorLayer)
111|6fd09e|        cursorLayers.append(cursorLayer)
112|27e597|    }
113|adc83b|
114|5a5008|    private func drawSelection(for range: NSRange, isPrimary: Bool, index: Int) {
115|2605b5|        guard let start = position(from: beginningOfDocument, offset: range.location),
116|cc2d91|              let end = position(from: beginningOfDocument, offset: range.location + range.length),
117|da2a96|              let textRange = self.textRange(from: start, to: end) else { return }
118|adc83b|
119|5d8027|        let selectionRects = selectionRects(for: textRange)
120|adc83b|
121|127303|        for rect in selectionRects {
122|433f1e|            let selectionLayer = CALayer()
123|f562d1|            selectionLayer.backgroundColor = (isPrimary ? selectionColor : secondarySelectionColor).cgColor
124|ce165e|            selectionLayer.frame = rect.rect
125|adc83b|
126|6930ca|            // Insert behind text
127|dc1f87|            if let textLayer = layer.sublayers?.first {
128|2b2195|                layer.insertSublayer(selectionLayer, below: textLayer)
129|f5a6eb|            } else {
130|1777fc|                layer.addSublayer(selectionLayer)
131|a7dc16|            }
132|6cbf28|            selectionLayers.append(selectionLayer)
133|5f3077|        }
134|27e597|    }
135|adc83b|

126|f905d2|## Troubleshooting Duplicate Warnings
127|adc83b|
128|586e24|If you see "keyboard shortcut already in use" warnings:
129|adc83b|
130|244022|1. Check that `VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift` does NOT define inline menu structs
131|1275d8|2. Check that the Menus/ folder files are the ONLY place defining these Commands structs
132|134003|3. Ensure `AppCommands.swift` is NOT included in `.commands {}` block

68|f2cec5|struct KeyCommandBridge<Content: View>: UIViewControllerRepresentable {
69|f160e2|    let content: Content
70|b4687f|    
71|ca8c99|    init(@ViewBuilder content: () -> Content) {
72|0bc2b5|        self.content = content()
73|27e597|    }
74|b4687f|    
75|5ed0a9|    func makeUIViewController(context: Context) -> KeyCommandController {
76|6b6e02|        let controller = KeyCommandController()
77|5a4a2c|        let host = UIHostingController(rootView: content)
78|0596a7|        host.view.backgroundColor = .clear
79|a81475|        controller.addChild(host)
80|285c40|        controller.view.addSubview(host.view)
81|e88a8e|        host.view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
82|c31f08|        NSLayoutConstraint.activate([
83|4f3c57|            host.view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: controller.view.topAnchor),
84|0bc6fc|            host.view.bottomAnchor.constraint(equalTo: controller.view.bottomAnchor),
85|fff93c|            host.view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: controller.view.leadingAnchor),
